  <script nonce="">
var form = function (cadena) {
    var chars = {
    "á": "a", "é": "e", "í": "i", "ó": "o", "ú": "u",
    "à": "a", "è": "e", "ì": "i", "ò": "o", "ù": "u", "ñ": "n",
    "Á": "A", "É": "E", "Í": "I", "Ó": "O", "Ú": "U",
    "À": "A", "È": "E", "Ì": "I", "Ò": "O", "Ù": "U", "Ñ": "N",
    "¡": "", "!": "", "¿": "", "?": "",
    }
    var expr = /[áàéèíìóòúùñ¡!¿?]/ig;      
    if (!!cadena){
    var res = cadena.replace(expr, function (e) { return chars[e] });
    } else {
    var res = "no aplica";
    }
    return res.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim().toLowerCase();
}
</script>

  <script type="module">
	import "https://entel.cdn.modyo.com/libraries/v1.5.5.1/src/components/lit-components/header/complete/web-component.min.js";

	window.addEventListener("load", () => {
		const searchBar = document.getElementById('btn-search-header');
		if (!searchBar) {
			console.error("No se encontró el elemento con el ID especificado.");
			return;
		}
		if (!searchBar.shadowRoot) {
			console.error("El elemento no tiene un shadowRoot.");
			return;
		}

		const inputElement = searchBar.shadowRoot.querySelector('input');

		if (!inputElement) {
			console.error("No se encontró el input dentro del shadowRoot.");
			return;
		}

		inputElement.addEventListener('keypress', (event) => {

			if (event.code === 'Enter' || event.key === 'Enter') {
				const searchQuery = inputElement.value;
				const encodedQuery = encodeURIComponent(searchQuery);
				const searchUrl = `https://www.entel.cl/buscador/resultados?cx=012036399463253452810:gizuw1e8ilq&cof=FORID:10&ie=UTF-8&q=${encodedQuery}`;

				window.location.href = searchUrl;
			}
		});


	});

</script>

   <script type="module" nonce="">
    window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
window.onload = function () {
    function watchElements(selector, callback) {
        var observer = new IntersectionObserver(function (entries) {
            entries.forEach(function (entry) {
                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                    callback(entry.target);  
                    observer.unobserve(entry.target);
                }
            });
        }, { threshold: 0.5 });

        var elements = document.querySelectorAll(selector);
        elements.forEach(function (element) {
            observer.observe(element);
        });
    }

    watchElements("section", function (element) {  
        var market = element.getAttribute('data-market') || undefined ;
        var section = element.getAttribute('data-section') || undefined ;
        var event_label = element.getAttribute('data-label') || undefined ;
        var location = element.getAttribute('data-location') || undefined ;
        var level_1 = element.getAttribute('data-level-1') || undefined ;
			  var variant_1 = element.getAttribute('data-variant-1') || undefined ;
        var event_action = element.getAttribute('data-action') || undefined ;
        var event = element.getAttribute('data-event') || undefined ;
        var event_category = element.getAttribute('data-category') || undefined ;
// si está vacio que arroje undefined
       if(event){
        dataLayer.push({
            "event": event,
            "event_category": event_category,
            "event_action": event_action,
            "event_label":event_label ,
            "section":section ,
            "level_1": level_1,
					  "variant_1": variant_1,
            "location": location,
            "market": market
        });
       }
    });
}; 
</script>

   <script type="module" nonce="">
    










let bannerVisible = false;

 window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
	 let scrollPos = 500;
	 const nav = document.querySelector('.eds-smartbanner');

	 let windowY = window.scrollY;
	 if (windowY < scrollPos) {
		 // Scrolling UP
		 nav.style.visibility = 'hidden';

	 } else if (windowY > 2800) {
		 nav.style.visibility = 'hidden';

	 } else {
		 // Scrolling DOWN
		 nav.style.visibility = 'visible';

		 // Solo ejecuta el dataLayer.push la primera vez que se hace visible
		 if (!bannerVisible) {
			 bannerVisible = true;
			 dataLayer.push({
				 'event': "load",
				 'event_label': "conectate con mas diversion a internet hogar desde $18.990",
				 'event_category': "home",
				 'event_action': "impressions",
				 'market': "pe",
				 'segment': "otros",
				 'section': "smart banner",
				 'location':"02"
			 });
		 }
	 }
 });
 
 
</script>

    const sub_section = "carrusel";
    const market = "pe";

    const buttons = bannerHero.getRootElements("btns"); // Usa tu método para obtener los botones

    let buttonData;
    
      if (slideChangeCount === 1) {
        buttonData = data_1;
      }
    
      if (slideChangeCount === 2) {
        buttonData = data_2;
      }
    
      if (slideChangeCount === 3) {
        buttonData = data_3;
      }
    
      if (slideChangeCount === 4) {
        buttonData = data_4;
      }
    
      if (slideChangeCount === 5) {
        buttonData = data_5;
      }
    
      if (slideChangeCount === 6) {
        buttonData = data_6;
      }
    

    const dataPush = {
      event: "load",
      event_category: "home",
      event_action: "impressions",
      event_label: "banner principales",
      variant_1: buttonData.variant,
      product_name: buttonData.productName || undefined,
      description: buttonData.description || undefined,
      position: buttonData.position,
      date: buttonData.date || undefined,
      section: buttonData.section,
      sub_section: sub_section,
      location: buttonData.location,
      market: market,
    };

    // Envía el dato al dataLayer
    dataLayer.push(dataPush);
  }

  // Función para manejar el evento de cambio de diapositiva
  function onSlideChange() {
    const currentIndex = swiperHome.activeIndex;
    const previousIndex = swiperHome.previousIndex;

    // Solo incrementar si es un cambio hacia adelante y la diapositiva actual no ha sido procesada antes
    if (
      currentIndex > previousIndex &&
      isVisible &&
      !processedSlides.has(currentIndex)
    ) {
      slideChangeCount++;
      processedSlides.add(currentIndex);

      if (slideChangeCount <= maxSlideChanges) {
        getBannerInfo();
      }

      // Si hemos alcanzado el máximo de cambios de diapositiva, eliminar el evento
      if (slideChangeCount >= maxSlideChanges) {
        swiperHome.off("slideChange", onSlideChange);
      }
    }
  }

  // Configuración del Intersection Observer
  const observerOptions = {
    root: null, // Usa el viewport como el contenedor de observación
    rootMargin: "0px",
    threshold: 0.1, // Ejecutar cuando al menos el 10% del contenedor sea visible
  };

  const observerCallback = (entries) => {
    entries.forEach((entry) => {
      if (entry.isIntersecting) {
        isVisible = true;

        const currentIndex = swiperHome.activeIndex;

        // Procesar la diapositiva actual si no ha sido procesada antes
        if (!processedSlides.has(currentIndex)) {
          getBannerInfo();
          processedSlides.add(currentIndex);
        }

        // Añadir el evento de cambio de slide si no se ha registrado antes
        if (!hasRegisteredSlideChange) {
          swiperHome.on("slideChange", onSlideChange);
          hasRegisteredSlideChange = true;
        }

        // Reanudar el autoplay del swiper
        swiperHome.autoplay.start();
      } else {
        isVisible = false;

        // Detener el autoplay del swiper
        swiperHome.autoplay.stop();
      }
    });
  };

  // Crear el Intersection Observer
  const observer = new IntersectionObserver(observerCallback, observerOptions);

  // Empezar a observar el contenedor del Swiper
  observer.observe(swiperContainer);


 
</script>

    bottom: 2px;
}

   <script type="module" nonce="">
    

  
  import "https://entel.cdn.modyo.com/libraries/v1.5.5.1/src/components/lit-components/label/web-component.min.js";




  
  import "https://entel.cdn.modyo.com/libraries/v1.5.5.1/src/components/lit-components/icon/web-component.min.js";


 import "https://entel.cdn.modyo.com/libraries/v1.5.5.1/src/components/lit-components/common/text-styler/web-component.min.js";



document.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
    const target = event.target.closest('a.gtm_link');
    if (target) {
        trackComponents(target);
    }
});




const mundoSectionPers = document.getElementById('mundos-pers');


async function getDataPers() {
    let params = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
    let cookieTest = params.get("cookie");
    try {
        const cookieMatch = document.cookie.match(/_ga=([^;]+)/);
        let cookieUser = "";
        if (!cookieMatch) {
            throw new Error("GA cookie not found");
        }

        if (!cookieTest) {
            cookieUser = cookieMatch[1].split(".").slice(2).join(".");
        }

        const postBody = {
            visitorId: cookieTest || cookieUser,
        };

        
        const url = "https://ecom-recommendation-ai.en.tel/api/search";
        

      
        const response = await axios.post(url, postBody);
				 
        let cardsContent = '';
        let smallCardsContent = '';
        let smallCardsContentSwiper = '';

      for (let i = 0; i < response.data.plans.length; i++) {
        try {
          const element = response.data.plans[i];
         
					let dataModyo = await axios.get(`https://altiplano.entel.cl/api/content/spaces/${element.categories}/types/ficha-producto-nuevo/entries?meta.slug=${element.id}`);
					
          const plan = dataModyo.data.entries[0];
          let title = 'Plan desconocido';
          let pricetag = 'Precio no disponible';
          let discount = 0;
          let price = 'Precio no disponible';
          let segment = '';
          let typeService;
          let detalleContendor = "";

          if (i === 0) {
            //obtener detalle de movil		

         if (plan.meta.space === "movil") {
    // Crear un arreglo de promesas para las solicitudes
    const detallesPromises = plan.fields['Detalles del Plan Card'].map((itemDetalle, index) =>
        axios.get(`https://altiplano.entel.cl/api/content/spaces/movil/types/${itemDetalle.content_type}/entries/${itemDetalle.uuid}`)
            .then(detalle => ({ detalle: detalle.data, index }))
    );

    // Ejecutar todas las solicitudes en paralelo
    const detalles = await Promise.all(detallesPromises);

    // Procesar las respuestas
    detalles.forEach(({ detalle, index }) => {
        if (index < 3) { // Limitar la cantidad de detalles a mostrar
            detalleContendor += `<div class="d-flex align-items-center mt-2">
                <andino-icons eds-type="transversales" eds-name="${detalle.fields['Nombre Ícono']}" eds-class="icon-xs-2"></andino-icons>
                <andino-text-styler
                    class="mb-0 ms-2 body_2-xs"
                    eds-text="${detalle.fields['Texto Intermedio']}"
                    eds-element="p"></andino-text-styler>
            </div>`;
        }
    });
} else {
    // Crear un arreglo de promesas para las solicitudes
    const detallesPromises = plan.fields['Detalles del Plan'].fields.map((itemDetalleWrapper, index) => {
        const itemDetalle = itemDetalleWrapper["Detalle"];
        return axios.get(`https://altiplano.entel.cl/api/content/spaces/hogar/types/${itemDetalle.content_type}/entries/${itemDetalle.uuid}`)
            .then(detalle => ({ detalle: detalle.data, index }));
    });

    // Ejecutar todas las solicitudes en paralelo
    const detalles = await Promise.all(detallesPromises);

    // Procesar las respuestas
    detalles.forEach(({ detalle, index }) => {
        const maxDetalles = plan.fields['Beneficio'].fields.length > 1 ? 2 : 3;
        if (index < maxDetalles) {
            detalleContendor += `<div class="d-flex align-items-center mt-2">
                <andino-icons eds-type="transversales" eds-name="${detalle.fields['Nombre Ícono']}" eds-class="icon-xs-2"></andino-icons>
                <andino-text-styler
                    class="mb-0 ms-2 body_2-xs limit-desktop"
                    eds-text="${detalle.fields['Texto Largo']}"
                    eds-element="p"></andino-text-styler>
            </div>`;
        }
    });
}


          }


          if (plan.meta.space === "movil") {
            typeService = plan.fields['Tipo de Plan'];
            title = plan.fields['Nombre del Plan'] || 'Plan desconocido';
            discount = plan.fields['Porcentaje Descuento Plan'] || 0;
            segment = 'po';
      //price = plan.fields['Precio Normal'] * (1 - (plan.fields['Porcentaje Descuento Plan'] || 0) / 100) || 'Precio no disponible';
						
						price = plan.fields['Precio Normal'] ? Math.round(plan.fields['Precio Normal'] * (1 - (plan.fields['Porcentaje Descuento Plan'] || 0) / 100)) : 'Precio no disponible';
						
						if(plan.fields['Meses de la oferta'] > 0 )
						{
											price = `$${price.toLocaleString('es-CL')}/mes x ${plan.fields['Meses de la oferta']} meses`;
						}else
						{
										price = `$${price.toLocaleString('es-CL')}/mes`;
						}


            pricetag = String(price).replace("/ ", "").trim();
          } else {
        		 typeService = plan.fields['Servicio']
    ? `${plan.fields['Servicio']} ${plan.fields['Tipo de Servicio']}`
    : plan.fields['Tipo de Servicio'];

            title = plan.fields['Nombre Plan'] || 'Plan desconocido';
            discount = plan.fields['Descuento Online'] || 0;
            segment = 'hh';
						if(plan.fields['Precio Descuento Online']){
							 price = plan.fields['Precio Descuento Online'];
						} else {
							 price = plan.fields['Precio Normal'];
						}					
						
					if(plan.fields['Meses Online'] > 0 )
						{
					price = `$${price.toLocaleString('es-CL')}/mes x ${plan.fields['Meses Online']} meses`;
						}else
						{
					price = `$${price.toLocaleString('es-CL')}/mes`;
						}
						
		
						
            pricetag = String(price).replace("/mes", "").trim();
          }

         			  discount = discount > 0 ? `${discount}% dcto.` : 'Sin descuento';
       

          if (i === 0) {
            // Generar los iconos dinámicamente a partir de los elementos del array
            let iconos = '';
				
            const beneficios = plan.fields['Beneficio'];
		 if(beneficios)
		{
            for (let dataBeneficio of beneficios.fields) {
							
              iconos += `<andino-icons eds-type="${dataBeneficio['Type'] ? dataBeneficio['Type'] : 'marcas'}" 
                         eds-name="${dataBeneficio['Icono']}" 
                         eds-class="icon-xs-4"></andino-icons>`;
            }
		}
			
let urlIntermedia;						
if(plan.meta.space == "movil")		
{
urlIntermedia =`https://www.entel.cl/planes/contrataciononline?id=${plan.meta.slug}&lineas=1&oda=home_1_card-destacada&gen=entel__home`;
}
else
{
urlIntermedia =`https://www.entel.cl/hogar/contrataciononline?id=${plan.meta.slug}&lineas=1&oda=home_1_card-destacada&gen=entel__home`;	
}
		
						
						
						
            cardsContent += `
              <div class="col-xl-8 col-lg-12 col-12 card-destacada">
                  <a href="${urlIntermedia}" class="card-mundos-pers gtm_link" data-market="pe" data-segment="${segment}" data-section="recomendados para ti" data-product-name="${title}" data-product-price="${pricetag}" data-position="${i + 1}" data-label="${typeService} ${title}" data-title="${typeService} ${title}" data-description="${discount} ${price}" data-element="card" data-action="click_to_action" > 
                     <div class="card p-4 shadow-sm h-100 ${plan.meta.space === "movil" ? 'bg-movil-main' : 'bg-hogar-main'} align-content-md-center">

                          ${discount !== 'Sin descuento' ? `<andino-label eds-text='${discount}' eds-color="${plan.meta.space === "movil" ? 'green' : 'green'}"></andino-label>` : ''}
                          <h3 class="title-card-big subtitle_2-xs mt-4">${typeService} <b>${title}</b></h3>
                          <p class="display-6 price-card mt-2 headline_3b-xs">${price}</p>
                          ${detalleContendor}

                          <div class="d-flex mt-2">
                              ${iconos} <!-- Inserta aquí los iconos generados dinámicamente -->
                          </div>
                      </div>
                  </a>
              </div>

              <div class="hidden-mob col-xl-4 col-lg-12 col-12 mt-xl-0 mt-lg-4 mt-4">`;
          }
          else {
						
let urlIntermedia;						
if(plan.meta.space == "movil")		
{
urlIntermedia =`https://www.entel.cl/planes/contrataciononline?id=${plan.meta.slug}&lineas=1&oda=home_1_card-${i}&gen=entel__home`;
}
else
{
urlIntermedia =`https://www.entel.cl/hogar/contrataciononline?id=${plan.meta.slug}&lineas=1&oda=home_1_card-${i}&gen=entel__home`;	
}
						
            smallCardsContent += `
                    <a class="card-mundos-pers gtm_link" data-market="pe" data-segment="${segment}" data-section="recomendados para ti" data-product-name="${title}" data-product-price="${pricetag}" data-position="${i + 1}" data-element="card" data-label="${typeService} ${title}" data-title="${typeService} ${title}" data-description="${discount} ${price}" data-action="click_to_action" href="${urlIntermedia}">
                        <div class="card card-mini p-3 shadow-sm ${i !== 3 ? ' mb-4' : ''} align-content-center">
                            ${discount !== 'Sin descuento' ? `<andino-label eds-text='${discount}' eds-second-text="${plan.meta.space === "movil" ? 'Planes Móviles 5G' : 'Internet Hogar'}" eds-color="${plan.meta.space === "movil" ? 'green' : 'green'}"></andino-label>` : `<andino-label eds-text="${plan.meta.space === "movil" ? 'Planes Móviles 5G' : 'Internet Hogar'}" eds-color='${plan.meta.space === "movil" ? 'green' : 'green'}' ></andino-label>`}
                            <h3 class="title-card-small body_3-xs mt-2">${typeService} <b>${title}</b></h3>
                            <p class="price-card headline_4b-xs mt-1">${price}</p>
                        </div></a>`;

            smallCardsContentSwiper += `
                   <swiper-slide>
                        <a class="card-mundos-pers gtm_link" data-market="pe" data-segment="${segment}" data-section="recomendados para ti" data-product-name="${title}" data-product-price="${pricetag}" data-position="${i + 1}" data-element="card" data-label="${typeService} ${title}" data-title="${typeService} ${title}" data-description="${discount} ${price}" data-action="click_to_action" href="${urlIntermedia}"><div class="card p-3 shadow-sm">
                            ${discount !== 'Sin descuento' ? `<andino-label eds-text='${discount}' eds-second-text="${plan.meta.space === "movil" ? 'Planes Móviles 5G' : 'Internet Hogar'}"  eds-color="${plan.meta.space === "movil" ? 'green' : 'green'}"" ></andino-label>` : `<andino-label eds-text="${plan.meta.space === "movil" ? 'Planes Móviles 5G' : 'Internet Hogar'}"  eds-color='${plan.meta.space === "movil" ? 'green' : 'green'}' ></andino-label>`}
                            <h3 class="title-card-small body_3-xs mt-4">${typeService} <b>${title}</b></h3>
                            <p class="price-card headline_4b-xs mt-2">${price}</p>
                        </div> </a> </swiper-slide>`;


          }

        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Error al obtener los datos de Modyo:', error);
        }
      }

        cardsContent += `${smallCardsContent}</div>`;
        
        if (response.status == 200) {
            mundoSectionPers.innerHTML = `
                <div class="container">
                    <div class="text-center mb-4">
                        <h2 class="headline_3-xs">Inspirado en lo último que viste</h2>
                        <p class="lead subtitle_1-xs">Planes recomendados para ti</p>
                    </div>
                    <div class="row g-4">
                        ${cardsContent}
                    </div>
                    <div style="overflow: hidden;" class="hidden-desk" >
                        <swiper-container
                            id="card-small-mundos"
                            navigation="true"
                            init="false"
                            class="col-12 py-4">

                      ${smallCardsContentSwiper}

                       </swiper-container>

                    </div>
                </div>`;


 const contenedorCards = document.getElementById("card-small-mundos");

     if(contenedorCards){

      // TODO agregar flechas de navegación
      const swiperCards = {
              slidesPerView: 1,
              spaceBetween: 0,
              autoplay: false,
              pagination: {
                  clickable: true,
              },
              breakpoints: {
                  1920: {
                      spaceBetween: 20,
                      slidesPerView: 4,
                  },
                  1440: {

                      slidesPerView: 4,
                  },

                  },

                      slidesPerView: 1.5,
                  },
                  768: {

                      slidesPerView: 1.5,
                  },
                  500: {
                      spaceBetween: 5,
                      slidesPerView: 1.5,
                  },
                  375: {
                      spaceBetween: 5,
                      slidesPerView: 1.5,
                  },
              },
              injectStyles: [
              `
                .swiper-wrapper {
                  align-items: flex-end;
                }

                swiper-container {
                  overflow: clip;
                  overflow-clip-margin:15px
                }

                .swiper-pagination {
                  position: sticky;
                  margin-top: 1rem;
                }

                .swiper-pagination-bullet {
                  width: 8px;
                  height: ext-align: center;
                  line-height: 20px;
                  font-size: 12px;
                  color: #000;
                  opacity: 1;
                  background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
                  margin-top: 2rem;
                }

                .swiper-pagination-bullet-active {
                  width: 32px;
                  border-radius: 12px;
                  color: #fff;
                  background:#002EFF;

                .swiper-button-next,
                .swiper-button-prev {
                  display: none;
                }

                .swiper-button-next.swiper-button-disabled,
                .swiper-button-prev.swiper-button-disabled {
                  opacity: 1;
                }

                }`,
              ]
          };

      Object.assign(contenedorCards, swiperCards);
      contenedorCards.initialize();
     }

        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error(`Error al obtener el RFM - ${error.message}`);
				mundoSectionPers.innerHTML = '';
        mundoSectionPers.classList.add('d-none');
    }
};
    getDataPers();

const andinoTabs = document.getElementById("tab-terminales-element");
const tabButtons = andinoTabs.getRootElements("tabs");
const buttonShowMore = andinoTabs.getRootElements("btn");

tabButtons.forEach((tabButton) => {
  tabButton.addEventListener("click", () => {
    const buttonText = tabButton.innerText.trim();
    const edsButton = JSON.parse(andinoTabs.getAttribute("eds-button"));

    edsButton.text = `Mostrar más ${buttonText.toLowerCase()}`;
    const activeCategory = categories.find(
      (category) => category.meta.name === buttonText
    );
    edsButton.href = activeCategory.fields["Link mostrar más"];

    edsButton.data.segment =
      buttonText.toLowerCase() == "celulares" ? "tm-equ" : "tm-acc";
    edsButton.data.title = `mostrar mas ${buttonText.toLowerCase()}`;
    edsButton.data.label = `mostrar mas ${buttonText.toLowerCase()}`;

    andinoTabs.setAttribute("eds-button", JSON.stringify(edsButton));
  });
});

   <script type="module">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    // Selecciona el botón específico por su id
    var boton = document.querySelector("#banner-action-btn");
		

    // Añade un evento click al botón
    boton.addEventListener("click", function() {
						
        // Selecciona todos los elementos cuyo className empiece con "card-carrusel-"
        var enlaces = document.querySelectorAll("[id^='card-carrusel-']");

        // Itera sobre todos los elementos seleccionados
        enlaces.forEach(function(enlace) {
            // Modifica la URL del enlace
					
enlace.href = enlace.href.replace("_section-ottp_card", "_beneficios-btn_card");
enlace.href = enlace.href.replace("_requisitos-btn_card", "_beneficios-btn_card");
						
					if(!enlace.href.includes('_beneficios-btn_card'))
						{
						 enlace.href = enlace.href.replace("_card", "_beneficios-btn_card");
						}
           
        });
    });
});
</script>

   <script type="module" nonce="">
    






	function watchCardsOTT(selector, callback) {
		var cardObserver = new IntersectionObserver(function (cards) {
			cards.forEach(function (card) {
				if (card.isIntersecting) {
					callback(card.target);  
					cardObserver.unobserve(card.target);
				}
			});
		}, { threshold: 0.5 });  

		var elements = document.querySelector('section.card-ott').querySelector('andino-card-ott').shadowRoot.querySelectorAll(selector);
		elements.forEach(function (element) {
			cardObserver.observe(element);
		});
	}

	watchCardsOTT("div.eds-card-ott", function (element) {
		var position = element.parentElement.getAttribute('aria-label').charAt(0);
		var raw_title = element.querySelector("andino-icons").getAttribute('eds-name');
		var raw_description = element.querySelector("andino-text-styler").getAttribute('eds-text');
		var raw_label = element.querySelector("andino-button").getAttribute('eds-text');

		var title = raw_title.replace(/-/g, '').replace(/0/g, '').replace(/2/g, '').replace(/logo/g, '').replace(/white/g, '').replace(/premium/g, '').replace(/plus/g, '').trim();
		var description = raw_description.replace(/í/g, 'i').trim();
		var label = raw_label.replace(/ó/g, 'o').trim();

		dataLayer.push({
			"event": "load",
			"event_action": "impressions",
			"event_category": "home",
			"event_label": label.toLowerCase(),
			"market": "pe",
			"section": "servicios de entretencion",
			"segment": "ott",
			"title": title.toLowerCase(),
			"description": description.toLowerCase(),
			"location": "09",
			"position": position,
		});
	});
 
 
</script>

		"altiplano.entel.cl",
	];

	const endpointzord = urlsToEndpoint.includes(window.location.hostname) ? "https://megazord.en.tel/api/" : "https://uat-megazord.en.tel/api/";

	const getRecaptchaToken = async () => {
		return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
			grecaptcha.enterprise.ready(async () => {
				try {
					const token = await grecaptcha.enterprise.execute(
						"6LcnDzAmAAAAALdKeZqdOXaWKMt7S4kJVKp0r1xW"
					);
					resolve(token);
				} catch (error) {
					reject(error);
				}
			});
		});
	};

	const enviaGenesys = async function(e) {
		let proceed = !0;
		const dateISO = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 19);
		const dateFormated = dateISO + "." + ('00' + new Date().getMilliseconds()).slice(-3) + "Z";

		const t = getCookie(e.origen + " " + e.tipo);
		return new Promise((async o => {
			if (t) {
				let e = dateFormated;
				const diffInMinutes = Math.round((new Date(e) - new Date(t)) / (1000 * 60));
				// moment(e).diff(t, "minutes") <= 2 &&
				diffInMinutes <= 2 && (proceed = !1,
															 o({
					status: "NOK",
					response: {
						descriptionDetail: "this user already has a request for the same product",
						code: 401
					}
				}))
			}else{
				proceed = !0;
			}
			if (proceed) {
				const t = await getMegazordToken()
				, n = await getRecaptchaToken();
				axios({
					method: "post",
					headers: {
						Authorization: "Bearer " + t
					},
					url: endpointzord + "genesys",
					data: {
						url: window.location.href,
						token: n,
						consulta: e
					}
				}).then((async function(t) {
					if (200 == t.data.result.code) {
						const n = {
							status: "OK",
							response: t.data.result
						};
						setCookie(e.origen + " " + e.tipo, dateFormated, .005),
							o(n)
					} else {
						const e = {
							status: "NOK",
							response: t.data.result
						};
						o(e)
					}
				}
								)).catch((async function(err) {
					400 == err.response.status && window.location.hostname;
					// setCookie(e.origen + " " + e.tipo, moment().format("YYYY-MM-DDTHH:mm:ss.SSS[Z]"), .005),
					// setCookie(e.origen + " " + e.tipo, dateFormated, .005),
					console.log('error en la peticion');
					const t = {
						status: "NOK",
						response: err.response
					};
					o(t)
				}
												 ))
			}
		}
											 )).catch((async function(e) {
			let t = e.response.data.message ? e.response.data.message : e.response.data;
			t = t + " endpointzord: " + e.response.config.url,
				e.response.status;
			const o = {
				status: "NOK",
				response: e.response
			};
			resolve(o)
		}
																))
	}
	, getMegazordToken = async function() {
		try {
			return (await axios.post(endpointzord + "token")).data.token
		} catch (e) {
			return !1
		}
	};
	function setCookie(e, t, o) {
		const n = new Date;
		n.setTime(n.getTime() + 24 * o * 60 * 60 * 1e3);
		let s = "expires=" + n.toUTCString();
		document.cookie = e + "=" + t + ";" + s + ";path=/"
	}
	function getCookie(e) {
		let t = e + "="
		, o = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie).split(";");
		for (let e = 0; e < o.length; e++) {
			let n = o[e];
			for (; " " == n.charAt(0); )
				n = n.substring(1);
			if (0 == n.indexOf(t))
				return n.substring(t.length, n.length)
		}
		return !1
	}

	async function generaSolicitud(dataPayload) {
		return void 0 !== dataPayload.mktOfferDescription && dataPayload.mktOfferDescription.length > 11 && (dataPayload.mktOfferDescription = dataPayload.mktOfferDescription.substring(0, 11)),
			void 0 !== dataPayload.mktOfferName && (dataPayload.mktOfferName = dataPayload.mktOfferName.toLowerCase(),
																							dataPayload.mktOfferName = dataPayload.mktOfferName.replaceAll("ñ", "n"),
																							dataPayload.mktOfferName.length > 50 && (dataPayload.mktOfferName = dataPayload.mktOfferName.substring(0, 50))),
			void 0 !== dataPayload.mktCampId && (dataPayload.mktCampId = dataPayload.mktCampId.toLowerCase(),
																					 dataPayload.mktCampId = dataPayload.mktCampId.replaceAll("ñ", "n"),
																					 dataPayload.mktCampId.length > 50 && (dataPayload.mktCampId = dataPayload.mktCampId.substring(0, 50))),
			"entel.digitalbeat.cl" == window.location.hostname && alert(JSON.stringify(dataPayload)),
			await enviaGenesys(dataPayload)
	}

const urlsToEndpointWhatsapp = [
    "www.entel.cl",
    "entel-promos.cl",
    "www.entel-promos.cl",
    "entel.cl",
    "promocionesentel.cl",

const endpointzordWhatsapp = urlsToEndpointWhatsapp.includes(window.location.hostname) ? "https://megazord.en.tel/api/" : "https://uat-megazord.en.tel/api/";

const getRecaptchaTokenWs = async () => {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        grecaptcha.enterprise.ready(async () => {
            try {
                const token = await grecaptcha.enterprise.execute(
                    "6LcnDzAmAAAAALdKeZqdOXaWKMt7S4kJVKp0r1xW"
                );
                resolve(token);
            } catch (error) {
                reject(error);
            }
        });
    });
};

const enviaWhatsapp = async function(payload) {
		let proceed = !0;
    const dateISO = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 19);
    const dateFormated = dateISO + "." + ('00' + new Date().getMilliseconds()).slice(-3) + "Z";

    const t = getCookieWs(`whatsapp ${payload.type}`);
    return new Promise((async o => {
        if (t) {
            let e = dateFormated;
            const diffInMinutes = Math.round((new Date(e) - new Date(t)) / (1000 * 60));
            // moment(e).diff(t, "minutes") <= 2 &&
            diffInMinutes <= 2 && (proceed = !1,
            o({
                status: "NOK",
                response: {
                    descriptionDetail: "this user already has a request for the same product",
                    code: 401
                }
            }))
        } else{
				  proceed = !0;
			  }
        if (proceed) {
            const t = await getMegazordTokenWs()
              , n = await getRecaptchaTokenWs();
            axios({
                method: "post",
                headers: {
                    Authorization: "Bearer " + t
                },
                url: endpointzordWhatsapp + "whatsapp",
                data: {
                    // url: window.location.href,
                    token: n,
                    number: payload.number,
                    type: payload.type
                }
            }).then((async function(t) {
                if (200 == t.data.result.code) {
                    const n = {
                        status: "OK",
                        response: t.data.result
                    };
                    setCookieWs(`whatsapp ${payload.type}`, dateFormated, .005),
                    o(n)
                } else {
                    const e = {
                        status: "NOK",
                        response: t.data.result
                    };
                    o(e)
                }
            }
            )).catch((async function(err) {
                400 == err.response.status && window.location.hostname;
                console.log('error en la peticion');
                const t = {
                    status: "NOK",
                    response: err.response
                };
                o(t)
            }
            ))
        }
    }
    )).catch((async function(e) {
        let t = e.response.data.message ? e.response.data.message : e.response.data;
        t = t + " endpointzordWhatsapp: " + e.response.config.url,
        e.response.status;
        const o = {
            status: "NOK",
            response: e.response
        };
        resolve(o)
    }
    ))
}
  , getMegazordTokenWs = async function() {
    try {
        return (await axios.post(endpointzordWhatsapp + "token")).data.token
    } catch (e) {
        return !1
    }
};
function setCookieWs(e, t, o) {
    const n = new Date;
    n.setTime(n.getTime() + 24 * o * 60 * 60 * 1e3);
    let s = "expires=" + n.toUTCString();
    document.cookie = e + "=" + t + ";" + s + ";path=/"
}
function getCookieWs(e) {
    let t = e + "="
      , o = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie).split(";");
    for (let e = 0; e < o.length; e++) {
        let n = o[e];
        for (; " " == n.charAt(0); )
            n = n.substring(1);
        if (0 == n.indexOf(t))
            return n.substring(t.length, n.length)
    }
    return !1
}

 async function generaSolicitudWhatsapp(e) {
    return void 0 !== e.mktOfferDescription && e.mktOfferDescription.length > 11 && (e.mktOfferDescription = e.mktOfferDescription.substring(0, 11)),
    void 0 !== e.mktOfferName && (e.mktOfferName = e.mktOfferName.toLowerCase(),
    e.mktOfferName = e.mktOfferName.replaceAll("ñ", "n"),
    e.mktOfferName.length > 50 && (e.mktOfferName = e.mktOfferName.substring(0, 50))),
    void 0 !== e.mktCampId && (e.mktCampId = e.mktCampId.toLowerCase(),
    e.mktCampId = e.mktCampId.replaceAll("ñ", "n"),
    e.mktCampId.length > 50 && (e.mktCampId = e.mktCampId.substring(0, 50))),
    "entel.digitalbeat.cl" == window.location.hostname && alert(JSON.stringify(e)),
    await enviaWhatsapp(e)
}

	window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
		let scrollPos = 100;
		const nav = document.querySelector('.eds-assisted-channels');

		let windowY = window.scrollY;
		if (windowY < scrollPos) {
			// Scrolling UP
			nav.classList.remove('pin');
			nav.classList.add('pin-hide');
		} else {
			// Scrolling DOWN
			nav.classList.add('pin');
			nav.classList.remove('pin-hide');
		}
	});

				}else{
					modalChannelsMovil?.setAttribute('eds-show', true);
					modalContratarMovil?.setAttribute('eds-show', true);
					
				}
				setTimeout(function() {
					dataLayer.push({
						event: "load",
						event_category: "movil - c2c topo",
						event_action: "info",
						event_label: "carga",
						segment: "po",
						section: "general",
						sub_section: "topo",
						location: "00",
						market: "pe",
						page_owner: owner,
						form_type: "c2c",
						journey_type: "solicitud",
						journey_name: "hogar"
					});
				}, 20);
			});
		}
				 
		if (catchOne) {
			catchOne.addEventListener("click", function() {
				applyModal('[eds-show="true"]');
				
					modalFab?.setAttribute('eds-show', true);
				
				
				
			});
		}
		if (catchOneMovil) {

				applyModal('[eds-show="true"]');
				
					modalFab?.setAttribute('eds-show', true);
				
				});
		}

		function validarNumeroTelefono(numero) {
			return /^[9]\d{8}$/.test(numero);
		}

		if (modalChannelsHogar?.shadowRoot) {
			let inputDataHogar = document.querySelector("[eds-id='input-llamame-hogar-desktop']");
			let btnLlamenHogar = document.querySelector("[eds-id='btn-llamame-hogar-desktop']");
			
			btnLlamenHogar.setAttribute("eds-disabled", true);

			inputDataHogar.addEventListener("input", (event) => {
				let value = event.target.value;

				if (value.length > 9) {
					value = value.slice(0, 9); // Corta el valor a los primeros 9 caracteres
					event.target.value = value; // Actualiza el valor en el input
					inputDataHogar.setAttribute("eds-value", value);
				}
				if (value.length === 9) {
					inputDataHogar.setAttribute("eds-success", "true");
					inputDataHogar.removeAttribute("eds-error");
					inputDataHogar.removeAttribute("eds-error-message");
					
					btnLlamenHogar.removeAttribute("eds-disabled");

				} else {
					btnLlamenHogar.setAttribute("eds-disabled", true);
					inputDataHogar.removeAttribute("eds-success");
					inputDataHogar.setAttribute("eds-error", "true");
					inputDataHogar.setAttribute("eds-error-message", "Ingrese un número de teléfono válido");
				}
			});
			btnLlamenHogar.addEventListener("click", async (event) => {

				btnLlamenHogar.setAttribute("eds-disabled", true);
				const numeroTelefono = inputDataHogar.value;
				if (!validarNumeroTelefono(numeroTelefono)) {
					inputDataHogar.removeAttribute("eds-success");
					inputDataHogar.setAttribute("eds-error", "true");
					inputDataHogar.setAttribute("eds-error-message", "Ingrese un número de teléfono válido");
					return;
				}

				const nowDate = new Date();
				const nowDateIso = nowDate.toISOString();
				const nowTime = {
					hours: nowDate.getHours(),
					minutes: nowDate.getMinutes(),
					seconds: nowDate.getSeconds(),
				};

					consulta: {
						origen: "publico",
						tipo: "hogar",

						mktOfferName: "",
						socialMediaId: "914470981.1723156920-1724389468",
						socialMediaName: "Publico - Hogar - Home",
						socialMediaSite: "10260045",
					}
				};
				modalChannelsHogar?.removeAttribute('eds-show');

				elementModalLoader?.setAttribute('eds-show', true);

					generaSolicitud(dataSendGenesysHogar.consulta)
						.then((data) => {
						switch (data.status) {
							case 'NOK':
								if (data?.response?.descriptionDetail === "this user already has a request for the same product") {
									//DATAPUSH
									const titleModalCurso = modalEnCurso.querySelector('.modal-header p');
									const textModalCurso = modalEnCurso.querySelector('#procesoModalTransversal p');
									const alertModalCurso = modalEnCurso.querySelector('#procesoModalTransversal eds-alerts');
									alertModalCurso.classList.remove('d-none');
									titleModalCurso.textContent = 'Te llamaremos pronto';
									textModalCurso.innerHTML = `Ya ingresaste una solicitud para contactarte. Recibimos tu información y te llamaremos lo más pronto posible.`;
									modalEnCurso.classList.add('show');
									setTimeout(function() {
										dataLayer.push({					
											event: "load",
											event_category: "hogar - c2c topo - conversion",
											event_action: "info",
											event_label: "carga",
											segment: "hh",
											market: "pe",
											page_owner: owner,
											status: "duplicidad", //exito error o duplicidad
											form_type: "c2c",
											journey_type: "solicitud",
											journey_name: "hogar",
											phone_client: btoa(numeroTelefono),					
											section: "general",
											sub_section: "topo",
											location: "00"
										});
									}, 20);

								} else {
									modalError.classList.add('show');
									setTimeout(function() {
										dataLayer.push({					
											event: "load",
											event_category: "hogar - c2c topo - conversion",
											event_action: "info",
											event_label: "carga",
											segment: "hh",
											market: "pe",
											page_owner: owner,
											status: "error", //exito error o duplicidad
											form_type: "c2c",
											journey_type: "solicitud",
											journey_name: "hogar",
											phone_client: btoa(numeroTelefono),					
											section: "general",
											sub_section: "topo",
											location: "00"
										});
									}, 20);

								}
								break;
							case 'OK':
								//DATAPUSH
								if (
									(nowTime.hours >= 9 && nowTime.minutes >= 0) ||
									(nowTime.hours <= 0 && nowTime.minutes < 1)
								) {
									document.getElementById("outOfTimeTransversal").classList.add("d-none");
									document.getElementById("successModalTransversal").classList.remove("d-none");
								} else {
									document.getElementById("outOfTimeTransversal").classList.remove("d-none");
									document.getElementById("successModalTransversal").classList.add("d-none");
								}
								const textModalSuccess = modalSuccess.querySelector('#successModalTransversal p');
								const alertModalSuccess = modalSuccess.querySelector('#successModalTransversal eds-alerts');
								alertModalSuccess.classList.remove('d-none');
								textModalSuccess.innerHTML = `Pronto te contactaremos al número que ingresaste. Te recomendamos mantener el teléfono cerca.`;
								modalSuccess.classList.add('show');

									dataLayer.push({					
										event: "load",
										event_category: "hogar - c2c topo - conversion",

								event_category: "hogar - c2c topo - conversion",

								const textModalSuccess = modalSuccess.querySelector('#successModalTransversal p');
								const alertModalSuccess = modalSuccess.querySelector('#successModalTransversal eds-alerts');
								alertModalSuccess.classList.add('d-none');
								textModalSuccess.innerHTML = `Pronto <span class="body_2b-xs">te contactaremos por WhastApp</span> a través del número que compartiste. Te recomendamos tener tu teléfono cerca.`;

								modalSuccess.classList.add('show');
							default:
								console.log("default");
								break;
						}
					})
						.catch((err) => {
						console.log("Error en la colicitud",err);
						setTimeout(function() {
							dataLayer.push({
								'event': "load", 
								'event_label': "carga",
								'event_category': " - ws topo - conversion", 
								'event_action': "info", 
								'market': "pe",
								'segment': "hh", 
								'section': "topo",
								'location':"00",
								'phone_client': btoa(numeroTelefono),
								'page_category': "landing-comercial", 
								'page_technology': "cms", 
								'page_owner': "hogar",
								'form_type': "ws",
								'journey_type': "solicitud",
								'journey_name': "hogar",
								'status': "error"
							});
						}, 20);

						modalError.classList.add('show');
					})
						.finally(() => {
						inputDataHogar.setAttribute("eds-value", 9);
						btnLlamenHogar.setAttribute("eds-disabled", true);
						inputDataHogar.removeAttribute("eds-error");
						inputDataHogar.removeAttribute("eds-success");
						elementModalLoader?.removeAttribute('eds-show');   
					});
				}

			});
		}
				 
		if (modalContratarMovil?.shadowRoot) {

			let inputDataMovil = document.getElementById('input-llamame-movil');
			let btnLlamenMovil = document.getElementById('btn-llamame-movil');
			let btnWspMovil = document.getElementById('btn-llamame-wsp');
			
			
			btnLlamenMovil?.setAttribute("eds-disabled", true);
			btnWspMovil?.setAttribute("eds-disabled", true);
			
			inputDataMovil?.addEventListener("input", (event) => {
				let value = event.target.value;

				if (value.length > 9) {
					value = value.slice(0, 9); // Corta el valor a los primeros 9 caracteres
					event.target.value = value; // Actualiza el valor en el input
					inputDataMovil.setAttribute("eds-value", value);
				}
				if (value.length === 9) {
					inputDataMovil.setAttribute("eds-success", "true");
					inputDataMovil.removeAttribute("eds-error");
					inputDataMovil.removeAttribute("eds-error-message");
					
					btnLlamenMovil.removeAttribute("eds-disabled");
					btnWspMovil?.removeAttribute("eds-disabled");

				} else {
					btnLlamenMovil.setAttribute("eds-disabled", true);
					btnWspMovil?.setAttribute("eds-disabled", true);
					
					inputDataMovil.removeAttribute("eds-success");
					inputDataMovil.setAttribute("eds-error", "true");
					inputDataMovil.setAttribute("eds-error-message", "Ingrese un número de teléfono válido");
				}
			});

				btnLlamenMovil.setAttribute("eds-disabled", true);
				btnWspMovil?.setAttribute("eds-disabled", true);
				const numeroTelefono = inputDataMovil.value;
				if (!validarNumeroTelefono(numeroTelefono)) {
					inputDataMovil.removeAttribute("eds-success");
					inputDataMovil.setAttribute("eds-error", "true");
					inputDataMovil.setAttribute("eds-error-message", "Ingrese un número de teléfono válido");
					return;
				}
				const nowDate = new Date();
				const nowDateIso = nowDate.toISOString();
				const nowTime = {
					hours: nowDate.getHours(),
					minutes: nowDate.getMinutes(),
					seconds: nowDate.getSeconds(),
				};

				const dataSendGenesysMovil = {
					consulta: {
						origen: "publico",
						tipo: "movil",
						startDateTime: nowDateIso,
						endDateTime: nowDateIso,

				};

				elementModalLoader?.setAttribute('eds-show', true);
				
				if(contactOptionSelected === 'c2c') {
					generaSolicitud(dataSendGenesysMovil.consulta)
						.then((data) => {
						switch (data.status) {
							case 'NOK':
								if (data?.response?.descriptionDetail === "this user already has a request for the same product") {
									//DATAPUSH
									modalEnCurso.classList.add('show');
									const titleModalCurso = modalEnCurso.querySelector('.modal-header p');
									const textModalCurso = modalEnCurso.querySelector('#procesoModalTransversal p');
									const alertModalCurso = modalEnCurso.querySelector('#procesoModalTransversal eds-alerts');
									alertModalCurso.classList.remove('d-none');
									titleModalCurso.textContent = 'Te llamaremos pronto';
									textModalCurso.innerHTML = `Ya ingresaste una solicitud para contactarte. Recibimos tu información y te llamaremos lo más pronto posible.`;
									setTimeout(function() {
										dataLayer.push({					
											event: "load",
											event_category: "movil - c2c topo - conversion",
											event_action: "info",
											event_label: "carga",
											segment: "po",
											market: "pe",
											page_owner: owner,
											status: "duplicidad", 
											form_type: "c2c",
											social_media_id: data.response.traceability_id,
											journey_type: "solicitud",
											journey_name: "movil",

											section: "general",
											sub_section: "topo",

										});
									}, 20);
								} else {
									modalError.classList.add('show');
								}
								break;
							case 'OK':
								//DATAPUSH
								if (
									(nowTime.hours >= 9 && nowTime.minutes >= 0) ||
									(nowTime.hours <= 0 && nowTime.minutes < 1)
								) {
									document.getElementById("outOfTimeTransversal").classList.add("d-none");
									document.getElementById("successModalTransversal").classList.remove("d-none");
								} else {

									document.getElementById("successModalTransversal").classList.add("d-none");

  <script defer nonce="">(async function registerServiceWorker() {
  if('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
    if('true' !== 'true') {
      await navigator.serviceWorker.getRegistration().then((registration) => {
        if(!!registration) registration.unregister();
      });
      return;
    }

    const swRegistered = await navigator.serviceWorker.getRegistration().then((registration) => !!registration);
    if(swRegistered) return;

    navigator.serviceWorker.register('https://www.entel.cl/serviceworker.js', { scope: '/'})
      .catch((e) => {
        console.error('Error during service worker registration:', e.message);
      });
  } else {
    console.warn('Service Worker is not supported');
  }
}());</script>
